[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocess through the LZMA tree checksum computation.[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere the program attempts to read from heap memory that has already been [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`treeck.[0m[1;92mc:33:20[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x5060000000a0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes into the freed region[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `compute_tree_checksum` [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m:  uint64_t block_width;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m:  uint64_t block_height;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m:  uint64_t block_size;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m:  size_t edge_count;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m:  struct TreeNode **edges;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m:  int state;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m for checksum cycle detection[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m TreeNode;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for Heap-Use-After-Free in Tree Checksum[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe critical issue is in `[0m[35m/src/xz/src/liblzma/check/[0m[95mtreeck.c[0m[39m` where the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`compute_tree_checksum` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m66[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m93[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m violates the separation of concerns [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprinciple by:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Mixing computation with cleanup**: Lines [0m[1;36m88[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m free the node and its edges [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray DURING the recursive traversal[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Premature deallocation**: After a recursive call to process a child [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m82[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat child node is freed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m89[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but the parent's loop continues and may [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess freed memory[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Cycle complications**: The tree structure includes backlinks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m53[0m[39m in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`create_tree`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m creating cycles, which exacerbates the use-after-free when nodes are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed while still referenced or in the call stack[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Evidence from AddressSanitizer[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **READ violation at treeck.[0m[1;92mc:79:34[0m[39m**: Parent loop accessing `node->edges[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter child has been freed[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **FREE at treeck.[0m[1;92mc:90:3[0m[39m**: The premature free operation[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **MALLOC at treeck.[0m[1;92mc:33:20[0m[39m**: Original allocation of the [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte TreeNode [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructure[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Multiple stack frames**: Multiple `compute_tree_checksum` entries confirm [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursive nature[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Reference Implementation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase provides the correct pattern in `src/liblzma/common/index.[0m[1;92mc:194[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m207[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `index_tree_node_end`:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Post-order traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchildren freed before parent[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Complete separation of processing from cleanup[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No memory access after deallocation[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove Premature Freeing from compute_tree_checksum[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File: `[0m[35m/src/xz/src/liblzma/check/[0m[95mtreeck.c[0m[39m`**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn the `compute_tree_checksum` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m66[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m93[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Remove lines [0m[1;36m88[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep all checksum computation logic intact [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function should ONLY compute the checksum value, not manage memory[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This ensures all nodes remain valid throughout the entire checksum [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation phase. Parent nodes can safely access child pointers after recursive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls return.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Dedicated Tree Cleanup Function[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File: `[0m[35m/src/xz/src/liblzma/check/[0m[95mtreeck.c[0m[39m`**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd a new static function `free_tree` immediately after the `compute_tree_checksum`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m93[0m[39m, before `lzma_tree`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Free the tree structure using post-order traversal[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic void [0m[1;35mfree_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTreeNode *node[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Handle NULL nodes[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!node[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only free nodes that were fully processed during checksum computation[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This prevents double-freeing in case of cycles [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbacklinks[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->state != STATE_HASHED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Mark node as being freed to handle cycles/backlinks[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Reuse the state field: STATE_CLEAR indicates [0m[32m"freed or being freed"[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    node->state = STATE_CLEAR;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Recursively free all children first [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpost-order traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < node->edge_count; ++i[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mfree_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Free the edges array and the node itself[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key design decisions**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **State-based cycle detection**: Checks `node->state != STATE_HASHED` to skip [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnodes that are:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Already freed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mencountered via backlink/cycle[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Not processed during checksum computation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshouldn't exist but defensive check[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **State marking**: Sets `node->state = STATE_CLEAR` before recursing to mark as [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"being freed"[0m[39m, preventing double-free[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Post-order traversal**: Frees children before parent, ensuring no parent [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccesses freed child memory[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **NULL safety**: Handles NULL child pointers gracefully[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Update lzma_tree Function[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File: `[0m[35m/src/xz/src/liblzma/check/[0m[95mtreeck.c[0m[39m`**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the `lzma_tree` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m95[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m102[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to add the cleanup phase:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextern [0m[1;35mLZMA_API[0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mlzma_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst uint8_t *buf, size_t size, uint32_t checksum[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned long seed = [0m[1;35mhash_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    TreeNode *root = [0m[1;35mcreate_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, size, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, seed, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    checksum ^= [0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mfree_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADD THIS LINE: Separate cleanup phase[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return checksum;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add `[0m[1;35mfree_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` call after line [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter checksum computation[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures: Create tree → Compute checksum → Free tree [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthree distinct phases[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to tree creation**: `create_tree` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m26[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m63[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged, preserving the backlink mechanism and tree structure[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to checksum algorithm**: `compute_tree_checksum` computation logic [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains identical, only removing the cleanup code[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to API**: `lzma_tree` signature and return value unchanged[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No changes to state tracking**: The STATE_CLEAR/VISITED/HASHED mechanism for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcycle detection remains functional[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Addresses All Issues[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Eliminates use-after-free**: Nodes are only freed after all traversal is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplete[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Handles cycles correctly**: State-based tracking prevents double-free via [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbacklinks[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Maintains memory safety**: Post-order traversal ensures children freed before [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparents[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No memory leaks**: All allocated nodes are properly freed[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Follows Codebase Patterns[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mirrors the `index_tree_node_end` pattern from [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/liblzma/common/index.[0m[1;92mc:194[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m207[0m[39m`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses post-order traversal for tree cleanup [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstandard pattern in the codebase[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reuses existing state field for cleanup tracking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconsistent with its design [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpurpose[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains separation of concerns [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomputation vs. cleanup[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No breaking changes**: The fix only modifies internal implementation, not [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal interfaces[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No test breakage**: Checksum computation remains bit-identical to original [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintent[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No performance impact**: Same number of tree traversals [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone for checksum, one [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor cleanup[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Memory usage**: Slight increase in peak memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree exists during checksum + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup instead of being freed during traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but this is negligible and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect behavior[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy is optimal because:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal invasive changes**: Only modifies the buggy file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges to headers, external APIs, or other components[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Proven pattern**: Uses the exact same post-order cleanup pattern already [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproven correct in the index.c implementation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Root cause fix**: Addresses the fundamental architectural flaw [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmixing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation with cleanup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than applying band-aid patches[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Cycle-safe**: Properly handles the cyclic graph structure created by backlinks[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Maintainable**: Clear separation makes the code easier to understand and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintain[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Defensive**: State checks prevent double-free even if the tree structure [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges in future modifications[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix transforms the code from:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Buggy**: Create → [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCompute + Free simultaneously with UAF bugs[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Correct**: Create → Compute → Free [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclean separation, no UAF[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis matches the design pattern used throughout the LZMA codebase for tree [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructure management and resolves the heap-use-after-free vulnerability completely.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
